<div class="Section0" style="LAYOUT-GRID:  16pt none">

# **<span style="FONT-SIZE:
 24pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 22.0000pt">附录B：怪物清单Monster Lists</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:
 24pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 22.0000pt"></span>**

</div>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY:
 黑体; COLOR:
 rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span>

<div class="Section1" style="LAYOUT-GRID:  16pt none">

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY:
 黑体; COLOR:
 rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">各环境中的怪物Monsters by Environmen</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY:

 'Times New Roman'; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">t</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY:

 'Times New Roman'; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"></span>**

<span style="FONT-SIZE:
 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"> 下列表格根据环境和挑战等级来组织怪物。这些表格省略了那些不习惯住在这些环境中的怪物</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:
 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">，</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:
 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">比如天使和魔鬼。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:
 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:
 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"></span>

 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">Arctic Monsters</span><span style="FONT-SIZE:

#### **<span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">草原怪物</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">Grassland Monsters</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"></span>**

#### **<span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">沼泽怪物</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">Swamp Monsters</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"></span>**

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">各挑战等级的怪物Monsters by Challenge R</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">at</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">ing</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"></span>**

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"> 该索引按挑战等级重新排列了</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">《怪物图鉴》</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">中的各怪物。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">

#### **<span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">挑战等级</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">0（0~10 </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">XP</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"></span>**

#### **<span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">挑战等级</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">23（50000 </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt">XP）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"></span>**
